## Category C — New Implementations (13 items)

### C-1: `labels_contains_caption` in `articles/persist.py`

Insert immediately before the `assign_article_to_label_filters` function (new function, after `apply_filter_actions`). This is a pure helper with no I/O.

```python
def labels_contains_caption(labels: list, caption: str) -> bool:
    """Return True if any label in *labels* has the given caption.

    Source: ttrss/include/rssfuncs.php:labels_contains_caption (lines 1098-1100)
    PHP: foreach ($labels as $label) { if ($label[1] == $caption) return true; } return false;
    Adapted: labels list elements are expected to be sequences where index 1 is the caption.
    """
    return any(lbl[1] == caption for lbl in labels if len(lbl) > 1)
```

### C-2: `assign_article_to_label_filters` in `articles/persist.py`

Insert immediately after `labels_contains_caption`. Depends on `label_add_article` (already imported inside `apply_filter_actions`).

```python
def assign_article_to_label_filters(
    session: Session,
    article_id: int,
    filters: list[dict[str, Any]],
    owner_uid: int,
    article_labels: list,
) -> None:
    """Assign an article to labels matched by label-type filter actions.

    Source: ttrss/include/rssfuncs.php (lines 1102-1113)
    PHP: foreach filters: if type=="label" and not labels_contains_caption: label_add_article
    Only assigns if the label is not already present in article_labels.
    """
    from ttrss.labels import label_add_article

    for action in filters:
        if action.get("type") == _ACTION_LABEL:
            caption = action.get("param", "")
            if caption and not labels_contains_caption(article_labels, caption):
                label_add_article(session, article_id, caption, owner_uid)
```

### C-3: `Article::completeTags` route in `blueprints/backend/views.py`

The `_rpc_complete_labels` handler (line 738) provides the exact pattern. The new handler belongs in the "Article class handlers" section (which does not yet exist — it will be a new section near the `_DISPATCH` table area). Since `Article::completeTags` and `Article::assigntolabel` / `Article::removefromlabel` all belong to `op=article`, create a new handler block.

The dispatch table at line 1295 needs three new entries added at the bottom of the `("rpc", …)` block: `("article", "completetags")`, `("article", "assigntolabel")`, `("article", "removefromlabel")`.

```python
# ===========================================================================
# Article class handlers — op="article"
# Source: ttrss/classes/article.php:Article
# ===========================================================================


def _article_complete_tags():
    """Return up to 10 tag completions matching a search prefix.

    Source: ttrss/classes/article.php:Article::completeTags (line-level)
    PHP: SELECT DISTINCT tag_name FROM ttrss_tags WHERE owner_uid = uid
         AND tag_name LIKE :search LIMIT 10, returns JSON.
    Adapted: R13 — JSON output.
    """
    from ttrss.models.tag import TtRssTag

    search = _param("search", "")
    q = (
        select(TtRssTag.tag_name)
        .distinct()
        .where(TtRssTag.owner_uid == current_user.id)
        .order_by(TtRssTag.tag_name)
        .limit(10)
    )
    if search:
        q = q.where(TtRssTag.tag_name.ilike(f"{search}%"))
    tags = db.session.execute(q).scalars().all()
    return jsonify({"tags": list(tags)})


def _article_assign_to_label():
    """Assign a list of articles to a label.

    Source: ttrss/classes/article.php:Article::assigntolabel
    PHP: calls labelops(true) → label_add_article for each article ID.
    """
    from ttrss.labels import label_add_article

    ids_str = _param("ids", "")
    caption = _param("caption", "")
    ids = [int(x.strip()) for x in ids_str.split(",") if x.strip().lstrip("-").isdigit()]
    if caption and ids:
        for article_id in ids:
            label_add_article(db.session, article_id, caption, current_user.id)
        db.session.commit()
    return jsonify({"status": "OK"})


def _article_remove_from_label():
    """Remove a list of articles from a label.

    Source: ttrss/classes/article.php:Article::removefromlabel
    PHP: calls labelops(false) → label_remove_article for each article ID.
    """
    from ttrss.labels import label_remove_article

    ids_str = _param("ids", "")
    caption = _param("caption", "")
    ids = [int(x.strip()) for x in ids_str.split(",") if x.strip().lstrip("-").isdigit()]
    if caption and ids:
        for article_id in ids:
            label_remove_article(db.session, article_id, caption, current_user.id)
        db.session.commit()
    return jsonify({"status": "OK"})
```

Dispatch table additions (inside `_DISPATCH`, after the `("backend", …)` entries):

```python
    # Article class operations — Source: ttrss/classes/article.php:Article
    ("article", "completetags"):     _article_complete_tags,
    ("article", "assigntolabel"):    _article_assign_to_label,
    ("article", "removefromlabel"):  _article_remove_from_label,
```

### C-4 through C-9: New CRUD functions in `prefs/feeds_crud.py`

These six functions all follow the existing pattern in `feeds_crud.py`: `session` first arg, SQLAlchemy `update`/`delete`, `session.commit()` inside.

Insert in a new `# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------` subsection after the "Access key management" block (after line 737).

**C-4: `remove_feed_icon`**
```python
def remove_feed_icon(session: Session, feed_id: int, owner_uid: int) -> bool:
    """Clear favicon colour data for a feed (icon removal).

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::removeicon
    PHP: UPDATE ttrss_feeds SET favicon_avg_color = NULL WHERE id = feed_id AND owner_uid = uid
    Returns False if feed not owned by this user.
    """
    if not verify_feed_ownership(session, feed_id, owner_uid):
        return False
    session.execute(
        update(TtRssFeed)
        .where(TtRssFeed.id == feed_id, TtRssFeed.owner_uid == owner_uid)
        .values(favicon_avg_color=None)
    )
    session.commit()
    return True
```

**C-5: `reset_pubsub`**
```python
def reset_pubsub(session: Session, feed_ids: list[int], owner_uid: int) -> int:
    """Reset PubSubHubbub subscription state to 0 for a list of feeds.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::resetPubSub
    PHP: UPDATE ttrss_feeds SET pubsub_state = 0 WHERE id IN (ids) AND owner_uid = uid
    Returns number of rows affected.
    """
    if not feed_ids:
        return 0
    result = session.execute(
        update(TtRssFeed)
        .where(TtRssFeed.id.in_(feed_ids), TtRssFeed.owner_uid == owner_uid)
        .values(pubsub_state=0)
    )
    session.commit()
    return result.rowcount
```

**C-6: `regen_opml_key`**
```python
def regen_opml_key(session: Session, owner_uid: int) -> str:
    """Regenerate the OPML publish access key for a user.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::regenOPMLKey
    PHP: calls update_feed_access_key('OPML:Publish', false, uid), returns new link.
    Delegates to update_feed_access_key with the canonical feed_id_str 'OPML:Publish'.
    """
    return update_feed_access_key(session, "OPML:Publish", False, owner_uid)
```

**C-7: `regen_feed_key`**
```python
def regen_feed_key(
    session: Session,
    feed_id: int,
    is_cat: bool,
    owner_uid: int,
) -> str:
    """Regenerate the per-feed access key.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::regenFeedKey
    PHP: regenerate per-feed access key, return new key.
    Delegates to update_feed_access_key with stringified feed_id.
    """
    return update_feed_access_key(session, str(feed_id), is_cat, owner_uid)
```

**C-8: `clear_access_keys`**
```python
def clear_access_keys(session: Session, owner_uid: int) -> None:
    """Delete all access keys for a user.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::clearKeys
    PHP: DELETE FROM ttrss_access_keys WHERE owner_uid = uid
    """
    session.execute(
        sa_delete(TtRssAccessKey).where(TtRssAccessKey.owner_uid == owner_uid)
    )
    session.commit()
```

### C-9: `addCat` route in `blueprints/prefs/feeds.py`

Insert in the "Category CRUD" section (after `rename_category`, around line 287). The `add_feed_category` function already exists in `ttrss.feeds.categories`.

```python
@prefs_bp.route("/feeds/categories", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def add_category():
    """Create a new feed category.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::addCat
    PHP: calls add_feed_category(trim(request["cat"]))
    """
    from ttrss.feeds.categories import add_feed_category

    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    cat_title = request.form.get("cat", "").strip()
    if not cat_title:
        return jsonify({"error": "title_required"}), 400
    created = add_feed_category(_s(), cat_title, owner_uid)
    _s().commit()
    return jsonify({"status": "ok", "created": created})
```

### C-10 through C-12: New routes in `blueprints/prefs/feeds.py`

These go in or after the "Access key management" section.

**C-10: `removeicon` route**
```python
@prefs_bp.route("/feeds/<int:feed_id>/icon", methods=["DELETE"])
@login_required
def remove_feed_icon(feed_id: int):
    """Clear the feed icon / favicon colour data.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::removeicon
    """
    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    ok = feeds_crud.remove_feed_icon(_s(), feed_id, owner_uid)
    if not ok:
        return jsonify({"error": "feed_not_found"}), 404
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})
```

**C-11: `resetPubSub` route**
```python
@prefs_bp.route("/feeds/pubsub/reset", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def reset_pubsub():
    """Reset PubSubHubbub subscription state for selected feeds.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::resetPubSub
    """
    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    ids_raw = request.form.getlist("feed_ids[]") or request.form.getlist("feed_ids")
    feed_ids = [int(x) for x in ids_raw if str(x).lstrip("-").isdigit()]
    count = feeds_crud.reset_pubsub(_s(), feed_ids, owner_uid)
    return jsonify({"status": "ok", "reset": count})
```

**C-12: `regenOPMLKey`, `regenFeedKey`, `clearKeys` routes**
```python
@prefs_bp.route("/feeds/keys/opml/regen", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def regen_opml_key():
    """Regenerate the OPML publish access key.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::regenOPMLKey
    """
    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    new_key = feeds_crud.regen_opml_key(_s(), owner_uid)
    return jsonify({"status": "ok", "access_key": new_key})


@prefs_bp.route("/feeds/<int:feed_id>/key/regen", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def regen_feed_key(feed_id: int):
    """Regenerate the per-feed access key.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::regenFeedKey
    """
    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    is_cat = request.form.get("is_cat", "false").lower() in ("1", "true", "yes")
    new_key = feeds_crud.regen_feed_key(_s(), feed_id, is_cat, owner_uid)
    return jsonify({"status": "ok", "access_key": new_key})


@prefs_bp.route("/feeds/keys/clear", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def clear_access_keys():
    """Delete all access keys for the current user.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/feeds.php:Pref_Feeds::clearKeys
    """
    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    feeds_crud.clear_access_keys(_s(), owner_uid)
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})
```

### C-13: `setplugins` route in `blueprints/prefs/user_prefs.py`

Insert after `clear_plugin_data` (after line 219). The `set_user_pref` import already exists in `save_config`.

```python
@prefs_bp.route("/user/plugins", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def set_plugins():
    """Save the list of enabled plugins as a comma-separated preference.

    Source: ttrss/classes/pref/prefs.php:Pref_Prefs::setplugins
    PHP: joins plugins[] array to comma string, calls set_pref("_ENABLED_PLUGINS", plugins)
    """
    from ttrss.prefs.ops import set_user_pref

    owner_uid = _owner_uid()
    plugins_raw = request.form.getlist("plugins[]") or request.form.getlist("plugins")
    plugins_value = ",".join(p.strip() for p in plugins_raw if p.strip())
    set_user_pref(owner_uid, "_ENABLED_PLUGINS", plugins_value)
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})
```

### C-14: `PluginHost.get_plugin_names`, `get_plugins`, `get_plugin` in `plugins/manager.py`

Insert after the `register_plugin` method (after line 443). These are simple dict-accessor methods on `PluginHost`.

```python
    def get_plugin_names(self) -> list[str]:
        """Return a list of all registered plugin names.

        Source: ttrss/classes/pluginhost.php:PluginHost::get_plugin_names
        PHP: returns array_keys($this->_plugins).
        """
        return list(self._plugin_registry.keys())

    def get_plugins(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        """Return a copy of the full plugin registry dict (name → instance).

        Source: ttrss/classes/pluginhost.php:PluginHost::get_plugins
        PHP: returns $this->_plugins.
        """
        return dict(self._plugin_registry)

    def get_plugin(self, name: str) -> Any:
        """Return the plugin instance registered under *name*, or None.

        Source: ttrss/classes/pluginhost.php:PluginHost::get_plugin
        PHP: return $this->_plugins[$name] ?? null.
        """
        return self._plugin_registry.get(name)
```

## Potential Challenges

1. **`_s().commit()` in blueprint routes for `add_category`:** The existing pattern in `blueprints/prefs/feeds.py` does not call `_s().commit()` in the route itself — that is done inside the CRUD function. The `add_feed_category` in `feeds/categories.py` does not commit (it just `session.add()`). The route must call `_s().commit()` explicitly, or `add_feed_category` needs a commit. Check whether other callers (e.g. OPML import) commit externally — if so, the route must commit, not the helper.

2. **`_article_complete_tags` CSRF exemption:** The PHP `Article::completeTags` is an autocomplete endpoint (read-only). Consider whether it belongs in `_RPC_CSRF_IGNORE`. The existing `completelabels` is already in that set — `completetags` should be added too.

3. **`regen_opml_key` / `regen_feed_key` duplication:** These are thin wrappers over the existing `update_feed_access_key`. If the audit script tracks them separately, the wrapper approach satisfies traceability without new SQL. If any caller expects a specific dict return shape (e.g. `{"link": …}` as PHP returns), the route may need to construct a public URL from the key.

4. **`assign_article_to_label_filters` vs `apply_filter_actions`:** There is overlap — `apply_filter_actions` in `persist.py` already handles `_ACTION_LABEL` inline. `assign_article_to_label_filters` is the PHP function called from the feed update path for pre-existing articles. The new function should not replace the inline logic in `apply_filter_actions`; it should be used as a standalone call for the re-score path.

name: session_2026-04-05

## Session Summary (2026-04-05)

Full coverage verification from scratch using tree-sitter call graph data.

### Problem Found

Previous "73/73 file coverage" claim used file-level matching — PHP files mentioned in Python, but individual functions within those files NOT individually verified. The `validate_coverage.py` had a fundamental limitation: 320 of 554 checked functions were "file-level matches" only.

### Solution Built

New tool: `tools/graph_analysis/exact_function_audit.py` — parses all Python Source: traceability comments in ALL formats (docstrings, `#` comments, line-number references, dot-notation, short paths, em-dash separators, hyphenated filenames) and cross-references against tree-sitter call_graph.json nodes for each PHP function.

### Audit Results (final)

| Metric | Count |
|--------|-------|
| In-scope PHP functions (L0-L10, non-3rd-party) | 458 |
| Exact / line-range match | 288 |
| Eliminated by spec/ADR | 170 |
| File-level only | **0** |
| Completely missing | **0** |
| **Exact+Eliminated coverage** | **100.0%** |

### Implementations Added (Category C — 13 new functions)

| Python Module | New Function(s) | Source PHP |
|---------------|-----------------|------------|
| `articles/persist.py` | `labels_contains_caption`, `assign_article_to_label_filters` | `rssfuncs.php` |
| `plugins/manager.py` | `get_plugin_names`, `get_plugins`, `get_plugin` | `pluginhost.php` |
| `prefs/feeds_crud.py` | `remove_feed_icon`, `reset_pubsub`, `regen_opml_key`, `regen_feed_key`, `clear_access_keys` | `pref/feeds.php` |
| `blueprints/prefs/feeds.py` | 6 new routes for the above | `pref/feeds.php` |
| `blueprints/prefs/user_prefs.py` | `set_plugins` | `pref/prefs.php` |
| `blueprints/backend/views.py` | `_article_complete_tags`, `_article_assign_to_label`, `_article_remove_from_label` + dispatch | `classes/article.php` |

### Eliminations Documented (Category B — 20 items)

Added to `ELIMINATED_BARE` in audit script and `# Eliminated:` comments in Python files:
- HTML dialog generators: `editfeeds`, `batch_edit_cbox`, `newrule`, `newaction`, `customizeCSS`, `toggleAdvanced`, `getHelp`, `printRuleName`, `printActionName`
- PHP ecosystem replacements: `get_dbh`, `run_hooks`, `load_all`, `ttrss_read/write/destroy/gc`
- stdlib/Flask replaces: `make_password`, `validate_csrf`, `sanity_check`, `getFeedIcon`, `geturl`, `convertUrlQuery`, `expire_lock_files`, `cache_images`, `add_feed_url`
- Entry-point files added to `ELIMINATED_FILES`: `ttrss/opml.php`, `ttrss/api/index.php`, `ttrss/public.php`, `ttrss/register.php`

### Source Comment Fixes (Category A — 25 items)

## Summary

**Root cause of the original gap:** The previous "73/73 files covered" claim used file-level traceability — PHP files mentioned somewhere in Python, but individual functions within those files not verified one by one.

**What was built:** `tools/graph_analysis/exact_function_audit.py` — a tree-sitter-aware exact function audit that handles all real-world Source: comment formats (docstrings, `#` comments, line-number ranges, dot-notation, short paths, hyphenated filenames, em-dash separators).

**Final audit result:** `458/458 = 100.0%` — 0 file-level-only, 0 missing.

| Change | Count |
|--------|-------|
| New Python functions implemented (Category C) | 13 |
| Source comments added/fixed (Category A) | 25 |
| Eliminated comments added (Category B) | 20 |
| Tests | 598 passed, 0 failed |
| Commits | 3 (`447e3d9`, `c42c599`, `4f72611`) |

**Docs updated:** `specs/09-source-index.md`, `memory/master_plan.md`, `memory/coverage_gap_plan.md`, `memory/MEMORY.md`, new `memory/session_2026-04-05.md`.
